    function sendAbTestingPageViewEvent() {
        if (window.hasOwnProperty('_gcol')) {
            const now = new Date().getTime().toString();
    
            const Ab = getCookieValue("AbTesting") || '';
            const msearchAb = getCookieValue("msearchAb") || '';
            const recoAb = getCookieValue("recoAb") || '';
            const janusAbTestCookieValue = Ab.split("|")[0];

            const abTestingCookieValue = [msearchAb, recoAb, janusAbTestCookieValue].filter(Boolean).join('-');
    
            if (!abTestingCookieValue) {
                return;
            }

            const eventData = {
                ts: now,
                channel: 'web',
                event: 'ty_analytics',
                tv007: '0',
                tv019: window.location.href,
                tv020: window.TYPageName || window.page_type || window.pageType,
                tv037: now,
                tv066: window.navigator.userAgent,
                tv230: 'WEBABTEST',
                tv231: 'ty_assignmentapi',
                tv232: janusAbTestCookieValue
            };
            
            window._gcol.Fire("ty_analytics", eventData);
        }

}

function sendOTRejectEvent() {
  if (!isBasketRemoveIgnored && window.hasOwnProperty('_gcol')) {
    const eventData = {
      event:"ty_analytics",
      channel:"web",
      pid: "7ef07174-643d-4f1c-adb6-a7628eb26b9b",
      sid: "76996f01-4989-491a-8176-86ae27d58f79",
      tv230:"SFWDISCO",
      tv231:"One_Trust",
      tv232:"click",
      tv266:"Reddet",
      tv267: window.TYPageName,
      tv021: window.document.referrer,
    };

    setTimeout(clearCookies, 1000);
    return window._gcol.SendWebBeacon(eventData, { isExternalBeacon: true })
  }
}

function OptanonWrapper() {
  try {
    const isAlertBoxClosed = _gcol && OneTrust.IsAlertBoxClosedAndValid();
    const isSeen = _gcol && _gcol.ReadCookie("AZ_SEEN") === "true";

    if ("True" === "True") {
      if (window && !isAlertBoxClosed && newPageCheckPages.includes(window.TYPageName)) {
        window.addEventListener("closeOTBanner", function () {
          OneTrust.Close();
          OneTrust.AllowAll();
          isBasketRemoveIgnored = true;
        });
      }
    }

    if ("True" === "True") {
      if (!isAlertBoxClosed) {
        var oneTrustBFCacheIgnoreHandler = () => {
          try {
            const isClosed = _gcol.ReadCookie("OptanonAlertBoxClosed");
            if (isClosed) {
              OneTrust.Close();
              OneTrust.AllowAll();
              removeEventListener("pageshow", oneTrustBFCacheIgnoreHandler);
            }
          } catch (e) {
            console.error(e.message);
            removeEventListener("pageshow", oneTrustBFCacheIgnoreHandler);
          }
        };
        addEventListener("pageshow", oneTrustBFCacheIgnoreHandler);
      }
    }

    OneTrust.OnConsentChanged(function (event) {
      isPerformanceCookieAccepted = event.detail.includes("C0002");
      if (isPerformanceCookieAccepted) {
        window.sessionStorage.setItem("OTFlowEvent",JSON.stringify({ tv266:"Kabul et", tv267: window.TYPageName}));

        let timeout = 0;
        if ("True" === "False") {
          window._gcol.AppendPixel({ event: "appstart", channel: "web" });
          timeout = 500;
        }

        window.hotjarManager?.start();

        setTimeout(() => {
          if (!isSeen) {
            document.cookie = "AZ_SEEN=" + "; Max-Age=0; path=/; domain=trendyol.com";
          }
          if (!isAlertBoxClosed && !isBasketRemoveIgnored) {
            window.location.reload();
          }
        }, timeout);

      } else {
        sendOTRejectEvent();
        clearCookies();
      }
    });
  } catch (ex){
    console.error(ex.message);
  }
}
